<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ge-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kunst.html>kunst</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-eld</i>.
</p>

***gelato.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gelato.html>gelato</a> (93182)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelato.html>gelato</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ice cream</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">gelātus</i>, derived from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">gelū</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">frost, chill</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gel-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cold</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelato.html>gelato</a></strong> (<i>usually uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">gelati</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">gelatos</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An <span class="Latn" lang="en">Italian</span> variant of <span class="Latn" lang="en">ice cream</span> made from <span class="Latn" lang="en">milk</span> and sugar, combined with other <span class="Latn" lang="en">flavourings</span>. The ingredients are <span class="Latn" lang="en">supercooled</span> while <span class="Latn" lang="en">stirring</span> to break up ice <a href = vnd.unilang:crystals.html>crystals</a> as they form.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">gelateria</span></li></ul>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:geld.html>geld</a> (158)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gheld</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ghelt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:geld.html>geld</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*geldą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">reward, gift, money</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʰeldʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pay</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:geld.html>geld</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">yield</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:geld.html>Geld</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">money</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">jild</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">gjald</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">payment</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌲𐌹𐌻𐌳</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gild</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tribute</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:geld.html>gelde</a></i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geld.html>geld</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of female animals</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> not pregnant
<dl><dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drachtig.html>drachtig</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of fish</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> male</li></ol>

***gelden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gelden.html>gelden</a> (7005)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelden.html>gelden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*geldan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*geldaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʰeldʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pay</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelden.html>gelden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to apply, to be applicable, to be in effect
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:minuten.html>minuten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stilte.html>stilte</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gelden.html>gelden</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hele.html>hele</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plaatsen.html>plaatsen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plechtigheid.html>plechtigheid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gehouden.html>gehouden</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The two minutes of silence <b>apply</b> throughout the whole <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:places.html>places</a> where no ceremony <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:held.html>held</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to count (be estimated as valid, useful, or influential)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be considered [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a></i> <span>(object)</span></span> = as], to be considered to be
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> Bataven <b>golden</b> in Vroeg-Romeinse <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a></b> elitetroepen.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The Batavians <b><a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> considered to be</b> elite troops in Early-Roman times.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

***geldkraan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:geldkraan.html>geldkraan</a> (42279)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geld.html>geld</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kraan.html>kraan</a></i>. Perhaps a calque, compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">money tap</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geldkraan.html>geldkraan</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geldkraan.html>geldkranen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geldkraan.html>geldkraantje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">economics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> money tap <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">metaphor for monetary stimulus by printing money</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span> <span class="defdate">[from mid 20th c.]</span></li>
<li>funding, source of money <span class="defdate">[from early 20th c.]</span></li></ol>

***geleider.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:geleider.html>geleider</a> (38292)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">geleidere</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geleiden.html>geleiden</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geleider.html>geleider</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geleiders.html>geleiders</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geleider.html>geleidertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>attendant, escort</li>
<li>conductor <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of heat or electricity</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> leader

***gelieve.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gelieve.html>gelieve</a> (11576)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelieve.html>gelieve</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention"> singular present subjunctive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">gelieven</i></span>, or <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">formal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> idiomatic construction
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:gelieve.html>Gelieve</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:receptie.html>receptie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:melden.html>melden</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Kindly</b> report to the reception.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>U</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gelieve.html>gelieve</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dezen.html>dezen</a> aangehechte <a href = vnd.unilang:formulier.html>formulier</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vullen.html>vullen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">May <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <b>respectfully ask</b> you to complete the form annexed hereto.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The verb <i>gelieven</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> mostly restricted to the third person singular of the present tense in the subjunctive mood, in which form it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not considered archaic, but rather as a formulaic expression indicating a polite, formal request. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> always accompanied by an infinitive introduced by <i><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i>. In such constructions, a non-finite clause functions as the subject, the direct object being <i><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a></i> (‘you’), which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> often elided. Hence, the literal translation of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gelieve.html>gelieve</a> X</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> ‘may it please you to X’.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:gelieve.html>gelieve</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:aanvoegende.html>aanvoegende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wijs.html>wijs</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> gelieven
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:gelieve.html>Gelieve</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bezoek.html>bezoek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gilīk</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*galīkaz</i>. Akin to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">alike</i>

<dl><dd>He <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> convinced that he <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>right</b>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>

***gelijken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gelijken.html>gelijken</a> (14244)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">geliken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gilīkon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*galīkōną</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ge-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijken.html>lijken</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelijken.html>gelijken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to resemble [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span>(object)</span></span>]</li></ol>

***geloof.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:geloof.html>geloof</a> (281)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelove.html>gelove</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gelôve</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gilōvo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*galaubô</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geloof.html>geloof</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geloven.html>geloven</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geloof.html>geloofje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>belief, conviction.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">religion</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> faith, religion.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The genitive form of the word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:des.html>des</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geloofs.html>geloofs</a></i>. Of its alternative form <i><a href = vnd.unilang:gelove.html>gelove</a></i> it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:des.html>des</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geloven.html>geloven</a></i> or <i><a href = vnd.unilang:des.html>des</a> geloves</i>. In Dutch, the genitive <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not commonly used outside of fixed expressions and literary language, but can be frequently encountered in early modern Dutch texts.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">belief<span class="ib-comma qualifier-comma">,</span> conviction</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:overtuiging.html>overtuiging</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">religion</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:godsdienst.html>godsdienst</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:religie.html>religie</a></span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bijgeloof.html>bijgeloof</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geloofsbelijdenis.html>geloofsbelijdenis</a></span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:geloven.html>geloven</a> (379)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gelôven</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gilōven</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*galaubijaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to believe, to hold valuable or pleasing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:geluk.html>geluk</a> (551)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">geluc</i>, further origin unknown. Found only in <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:West Germanic languages">West Germanic</a></span>.  More at <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Glück</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">joy, bliss, luck</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>
<ol><li>luck, good luck</li>
<li>happiness</li></ol>

***gelukkig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkig.html>gelukkig</a> (466)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">geluckig</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geluk.html>geluk</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkig.html>gelukkig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkiger.html>gelukkiger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkigst.html>gelukkigst</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>happy</li>
<li>pleased, satisfied</li>
<li>lucky</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkige.html>gelukkige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verjaardag.html>verjaardag</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkig.html>Gelukkig</a> Nieuwjaar</span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Indefinite adjectives describing people often remain uninflected, if they express a personal quality. This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not stylistically neutral, but <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a formal, rhetorical or poetic <a href = vnd.unilang:ring.html>ring</a> to it, and can occasionally distinguish literal meanings of an adjective from a more figurative one. Furthermore, this <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> only done with some nouns, not all. Hence, besides the regularly inflected "<a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkige.html>gelukkige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>", the uninflected "<a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkig.html>gelukkig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>" can also be encountered.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkig.html>gelukkig</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>luckily</li>
<li>thankfully</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkig.html>gelukkig</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li>in <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> tevredene <a href = vnd.unilang:toestand.html>toestand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voelen.html>voelen</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i>"<a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>Veel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mensen.html>mensen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vergissen.html>vergissen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkig.html>gelukkig</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:maakt.html>maakt</a>" <sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup></i> </li></ul></dd>
<dd><span style="color:0060ff;font-weight: bold;">▸</span> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hemel.html>hemel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zomer.html>zomer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verjaagt.html>verjaagt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zuur.html>zuur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stad.html>stad</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zong.html>zong</a> Charles Trenet <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a>: '<a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>Wij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkig.html>gelukkig</a></b>, Route <a href = vnd.unilang:nationale.html>Nationale</a> 7.'</i><sup id="cite_ref-Route_Nationale_7,_leuker_dan_de_Route_du_Soleil_3-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-Route_Nationale_7,_leuker_dan_de_Route_du_Soleil-3"> | 3 | </a></sup></dd></dl></li></ol>
